# ![SoftBank](../img/softbank_logo.svg "SoftBank logo") (ソフトバンク) #

Emojipedia now documents at the last released set of [SoftBank](http://emojipedia.org/softbank/) emojis, 
but there were many minor updates or vendor differences before their switch to Android and Apple emojis in 2016.

Encoding
--------

SoftBank emojis were traditionally organized in 6 JIS(?) tables labeled 
`G` (U+E0*xy*), `E` (U+E1*xy*), `F` (U+E2*xy*), `O` (U+E3*xy*), `P` (U+E4*xy*), `Q` (U+E5*xy*). 
Their cells occupied by emojis, *xy*, run from hexadecimal 21 through 7A (max). 
The JIS escape code sequence has the uppercase letter followed by the printable ASCII character for the respective 2-digit position U+00*xy*.
Shift-JIS codes run from hexadecimal F741 (E-21) through FBDE (Q-5E).
Unicode PUA code points used are U+E001..U+E53E, i.e. offset by -0x20.

Compatibility listings
----------------------

`http://mb.softbank.jp/mb/s/campaign/pictogram/{provider}/image/{category}/E{3 uppercase hexadecimal digits}_20.gif`, 
`provider: {au|docomo}`, `category: {kaomoji|event|tool|kimochi[12]|sports_game|shumi|tatemono_chizu|tenki|tabemono_nomimono|jinbutsu_chara|sizen|norimono|kigou[12]|doubutsu|fashion_beauty|kokki}`. 
Some (animated?) emoji are in a subfolder with the same name as the file name without extension.

Evolution
---------

- Softbank updated some emoji graphics in mid-2008.
  [![Overview of changed emojis.](index_pic_03.png)](https://www.softbank.jp/corp/group/sbm/news/press/2008/20080603_03/ "press release 2008-06-03")

## [epad](epad/) ##

- Source: J-Phone epad archive
- Original folder name: `j`
- 15×15
- 480 graphics
- File names: single letter `E`..`Q` followed by two hexadecimal digits `21`..`7F`
- Date: 2002

### [png](epad/png/) ###

- converted from original GIF files above

## [j](j/) ##

- Source: [Mobile emoticon support BBS (SmallPICT)](http://wap2.jp/download/spict/index.html)
- GIF
- 15×15
- 480 graphics
- File names: 4 hexadecimal digits `4F21`..`5159` 
  (the final two digits seem to somewhat correspond with JIS codes above)
  
The files in `epad` and `j` may be the same except for their file names. 
This has not yet been checked sufficently.

## [PicCharacter](pic-character/) ##

- Source: J-SKY editor (`editor_inst.exe/editor_inst/Programs/PicCharacter/`)
- GIF
- 16×16 or smaller
- 267 graphics plus 1 empty template
- File names: 3 decimal digits with leading zeros `001`..`267`

## [RareSets](rare/) ##

- Source: Extracted from Device User Guide PDFs
- 902SH https://cdn.softbank.jp/en/mobile/set/data/support/users-guide/shared/vf902sh/902sh-e-manual.pdf
- 702MO http://broadband.mb.softbank.jp/mb/japanese/mysoftbank/crm/online_manual/pdf/702mo/702mo.pdf
- 931SC https://cdn.softbank.jp/mobile/set/data/support/product/931sc/download/pdf/931sc_en_userguide_r4.pdf
- Not much known about these... They don't follow the normal generation of designs. 
- Missing color including the animated frames. 

## [tech](tech/) ##

- Source: `http://creation.mb.softbank.jp/mc/tech/tech_pic/img/`
- GIF
- 20×20
- 471 graphics, 59 of them animated
- File names: include 3 uppercase hexadecimal digits `{xyz}`, 
  possibly relating to Unicode PUA codes
  - still image: `E{xyz}_20.gif`
  - animated: `E{xyz}_20_ani.gif`
    * E101..8
    * E10D..F
    * E113, 5, 7, B, D
    * E12B
    * E130
    * E201, 6
    * E219
    * E30C
    * E310..3, 7, E..F
    * E320, 5..9, E
    * E335..7
    * E34B
    * E409, D
    * E412, 7, C, E..F
    * E422..3, 8..9, D
    * E433, 7, E
    * E440, 2, 7, B
    * E51F
  - missing: E254..A, E538..E
    * E254_20.gif
    * E255_20.gif
    * E256_20.gif
    * E257_20.gif
    * E258_20.gif
    * E259_20.gif
    * E25A_20.gif
    * E538_20.gif
    * E539_20.gif
    * E53A_20.gif
    * E53B_20.gif
    * E53C_20.gif
    * E53D_20.gif
    * E53E_20.gif
